  • laptop crashed = laptop travou/quebrou
  • restart = reiniciar
  • attachment = anexo (de email)
  • virus = vírus
  • toolbar = barra de ferramentas
  • Silly me! = Que bobagem minha! / Que burrice!

FRASES-CHAVE:

  1. "Can you help me with something?" → Você pode me ajudar com algo?
  2. "The printer won't work." → A impressora não está funcionando.
  3. "My laptop crashed." → Meu laptop travou.
  4. "Don't open the attachment." → Não abra o anexo.
  5. "Silly me!" → Que bobagem minha!

CENA 16 — Dr. Cheer e o Blues da Marie

Situação: Marie está se sentindo para baixo e Paul tenta animá-la com seu método peculiar.
Nível: Intermediário
Tema: Emoções, expressões idiomáticas, humor

DIÁLOGO:

— Marie, you've been so quiet. Are you okay?
— I'm just a little down in the dumps.
— Oh, I'm sorry. We've been arguing about colors and you're feeling blue.
— Blue?
— What's wrong, Marie?
— I don't know. I can't put my finger on it. I've just been feeling out of sorts.
— Don't worry! Dr. Cheer is here!
— Doctor who?
— At school, people call me "Dr. Cheer" because I'm always happy and I enjoy cheering people up!
— How do you do that?
— I practice laughing every day!
— Laughing at what?
— Nothing! I just choose to laugh.
— You just decide to laugh?
— I can't do that. It's not in my nature.
— How do you know? Just try. Let me hear you laugh.
— Ha.
— Louder.
— Ha ha.
— Come on. Keep laughing.
[laughter]
— You're right. It's not your personality.
— What now, Dr. Cheer?
— Chocolate. Works every time.

VOCABULÁRIO DA CENA:

  • down in the dumps = pra baixo / na fossa
  • feeling blue = se sentindo triste / com o blues
  • I can't put my finger on it = não consigo identificar / não sei explicar
  • out of sorts = indisposto / não estou bem
  • cheer people up = animar as pessoas
  • it's not in my nature = não é minha natureza
  • works every time = funciona sempre

FRASES-CHAVE:

  1. "I'm feeling a little down in the dumps." → Estou me sentindo um pouco pra baixo.
  2. "I can't put my finger on it." → Não consigo identificar.
  3. "I've been feeling out of sorts." → Tenho me sentido fora do normal.
  4. "Choose to laugh." → Escolha rir.
  5. "Works every time!" → Funciona sempre!

EXPRESSÕES IDIOMÁTICAS DESTA CENA:

  • down in the dumps = triste, desanimado
  • feeling blue = triste (blue = azul = tristeza em inglês)
  • out of sorts = não se sentindo bem, irritado
  • can't put my finger on it = não consigo identificar o problema

CENA 17 — Arte no Escritório

Situação: Miss Novak traz obras de arte para decorar o escritório e revela o talento fotográfico de Bob.
Nível: Intermediário
Tema: Arte, opiniões, expressões de apreciação

DIÁLOGO:

— Here's the painting. It was painted by a Russian artist. It's called "Sun on the Water."
— The artist was inspired by looking at the sea.
— What do you think?
— I think I could do that.
— It's fantastic!
— How interesting.
— It's very blue.
— Yes, it's gorgeous.
— Here's the sculpture. It was made by a British sculptor. It's called "City of Gold."
— Is it really gold?
— No, it's made of wood. It was painted gold.
— What do you think?
— It's cool!
— I think it would look good in your office.
— I think I prefer the painting. I'm fascinated by it.
— And here's the photograph. It's called "Winter." It was photographed in Paris.
— There's nothing there. It's a photograph of snow in a park.
[Bob shows his own photo]
— Hey, look! I'm an artist! Here's my latest work. It's called "Office Wall."
— I was inspired by looking at the walls of the office.
— I'm not so crazy about that one... but I do like what you've done here.
— I'm very moved by it, actually. It's a fascinating mixture of Eastern and Western traditions.
— You have talent.
— I do?
— I think I could sell this.

VOCABULÁRIO DA CENA:

  • painting = pintura / quadro
  • sculpture = escultura
  • photographer = fotógrafo
  • inspired by = inspirado por
  • fascinated by = fascinado por
  • I'm moved by it = estou emocionado por isso
  • I'm crazy about = sou louco por / adoro
  • talent = talento

FRASES-CHAVE:

  1. "What do you think?" → O que você acha?
  2. "I'm fascinated by it." → Estou fascinado com isso.
  3. "I'm not so crazy about that one." → Não sou muito fã desse.
  4. "I'm very moved by it." → Estou muito emocionado com isso.
  5. "You have talent!" → Você tem talento!

CENA 18 — Exercício no Escritório

Situação: Bob tenta se exercitar no escritório durante o trabalho.
Nível: Iniciante-Intermediário
Tema: Exercício, saúde, trabalho

DIÁLOGO:

— What are you doing?
— I'm exercising.
— Don't you have some work to do?
— I am working! I'm working and exercising.
— What work are you doing?
— I'm thinking. About ideas for Mrs. Batty's vacation.
— And what are you thinking?
— Beach vacation.
— I have to finish this. Can you go exercise somewhere else?
— No problem.
[Later]
— What are you doing?
— I'm getting in shape.
— Why are you doing that here? Why don't you go to a gym, or the park, or outside, or home?
— I don't have time to go to the gym.
— I can't work when you do that. Can you go over there?
— No.
[Later — running in the office]
— Bob! What are you doing?
— I'm working.
— Then why are you running?
— To get in shape. Running burns a lot of calories.
— Exercise later. Work now. Please.
— Yes, sir.

VOCABULÁRIO DA CENA:

  • getting in shape = ficando em forma
  • burn calories = queimar calorias
  • gym = academia
  • exercise = exercitar / exercício
  • work out = treinar
  • I don't have time = não tenho tempo

FRASES-CHAVE:

  1. "I'm getting in shape." → Estou ficando em forma.
  2. "Running burns a lot of calories." → Correr queima muitas calorias.
  3. "Can you go somewhere else?" → Você pode ir em outro lugar?
  4. "Exercise later. Work now." → Exercite depois. Trabalhe agora.
  5. "I don't have time to go to the gym." → Não tenho tempo de ir à academia.

CENA 19 — A Festa de Aniversário do Mr. Evans

Situação: A equipe planeja a festa de aniversário do chefe de forma colaborativa.
Nível: Intermediário
Tema: Planejamento, preferências, trabalho em equipe

DIÁLOGO:

— I've asked Cheryl to plan a party for Mr. Wells's group next Friday.
— Marie, I'd like you to choose the restaurant for the party.
— I'd love to!
— Bob, I'll let you choose the... you will?
— Paul, could you plan the music?
— Yes, good.
— I called 10 restaurants and had them give us a price for a party room.
— These two had the best prices. The Green Room is a nice restaurant.
— That's my favorite too!
— Now, Bob. About the food. I was thinking steak and potatoes.
— Well, the client asked for fish or chicken, so I had the restaurant put together a menu.
— Which do you like better?
— I like chicken more than fish, I guess.
— Great! Chicken it is.
— Now, Paul. Let me guess — you have a list of music choices.
— Yes.
— These look fine. I think we're all done.
— You see how easy it is to plan something when we do it all together?

VOCABULÁRIO DA CENA:

  • plan a party = planejar uma festa
  • party room = salão para festas
  • put together a menu = montar um menu
  • Which do you like better? = Qual você prefere?
  • Chicken it is! = Frango então! / Decidido: frango!
  • work together = trabalhar juntos

FRASES-CHAVE:

  1. "I'd like you to ___." → Quero que você ___.
  2. "Which do you like better?" → Qual você prefere?
  3. "___ it is!" → Decidido: ___! / ___ então!
  4. "How easy it is when we work together!" → Como é fácil quando trabalhamos juntos!
  5. "Could you plan the music?" → Você poderia planejar a música?

CENA 20 — Planejando o Casamento

Situação: Bob e Cheryl não conseguem concordar em nada para o casamento deles.
Nível: Intermediário-Avançado
Tema: Casamento, negociação, compromisso

DIÁLOGO:

— I didn't know planning a wedding would be so hard.
— How many people should we invite?
— Bob wants a small wedding — 20 guests.
— I want a large wedding — about 300 people.
— Yesterday you said 200.
— I have a lot of relatives who want to come.
— Then there's the location.
— I always thought I'd get married in a park or at the beach.
— I would like to get married indoors, where I won't get wet if it's raining.
— I prefer traditional music in the ceremony.
— Contemporary music!
— I'd like a long ceremony and a short reception.
— I want a short ceremony and a huge celebration afterwards!
— I want a white cake.
— And I want a chocolate cake!
— How are we ever going to agree on this?
[Marie's solution:]
— Plan a wedding that's big enough to include all of Cheryl's family.
— In the park on Oak Street — that has a building where you can go if it rains.
— You can have traditional music in the ceremony and contemporary music at the party.
— And you could have two cakes at the reception — one white and one chocolate.
— Sounds okay to me.
— Me too!
— We did it!

VOCABULÁRIO DA CENA:

  • guests = convidados
  • relatives = parentes
  • ceremony = cerimônia
  • reception = recepção
  • indoors = em local fechado / interno
  • compromise = compromisso / meio-termo
  • agree = concordar

FRASES-CHAVE:

  1. "How are we ever going to agree?" → Como vamos chegar a um acordo?
  2. "I always thought I'd ___." → Sempre pensei que ia ___.
  3. "Where I won't get wet." → Onde não vou me molhar.
  4. "Sounds okay to me." → Parece bom pra mim.
  5. "We did it!" → Conseguimos!

MÓDULO 2 — MÚSICAS DO VÍDEO

Letra + tradução + vocabulário + o que aprender

MÚSICA 01 — "Everything Will Be All Right"

Tema: Saindo à noite, planos, entretenimento
Estilo: Pop / Musical

TRECHO PRINCIPAL:

Everything will be all right
When you and I go out tonight.
Where Thomas So gives us talk — the famous chef.
That's not for me.
The doors open at 9:00.
There's a movie we could see
Smith and Second Avenue —
That's my favorite neighborhood.
I can't wait to be with you.
I can't wait to have some food.
Everything will be all right
When you and I go out tonight.

TRADUÇÃO:

Tudo vai ficar bem
quando você e eu sairmos hoje à noite.
Não me interessa.
As portas abrem às 21h.
Tem um filme que poderíamos ver
na Smith com a Second Avenue —
Esse é meu bairro favorito.
Mal posso esperar para estar com você.
Mal posso esperar para comer alguma coisa.
Tudo vai ficar bem
quando você e eu sairmos hoje à noite.

VOCABULÁRIO DA MÚSICA:

  • everything will be all right = tudo vai ficar bem
  • go out = sair
  • That's not for me = Não é para mim / Não me interessa
  • I can't wait to = Mal posso esperar para / Estou ansioso para
  • favorite neighborhood = bairro favorito

FRASES-CHAVE PARA USAR:

  1. "Everything will be all right." → Tudo vai ficar bem.
  2. "I can't wait to ___." → Mal posso esperar para ___.
  3. "That's not for me." → Não é para mim.
  4. "Let's go out tonight." → Vamos sair hoje à noite.

MÚSICA 02 — "On My Dream Vacation"

Tema: Viagem, romance, sonhos
Estilo: Balada pop

TRECHO PRINCIPAL:

The ride was bumpy and much too long.
It was pretty boring. It felt so wrong.
I slept all night and it rained all day.
We left the road and we lost the way.
Then you came along and you took my hand.
You whispered words I could understand.
On my dream vacation, I dream of you.
I don't ever want to wake up.
On my dream vacation, this much is true —
I don't ever want it to stop.

The food was awful. They stole my purse.
The whole two weeks went from bad to worse.
They cancelled my ticket. I missed my flight.
They were so unfriendly. It just wasn't right.
So I called a taxi and I got inside —
And there you were, sitting by my side.

VOCABULÁRIO DA MÚSICA:

  • bumpy = cheio de solavancos / turbulento
  • boring = chato / entediante
  • lost the way = perdeu o caminho
  • whispered = sussurrou
  • dream vacation = férias dos sonhos
  • from bad to worse = de mal a pior
  • cancelled = cancelado
  • missed my flight = perdi meu voo
  • unfriendly = antipático
  • sitting by my side = sentado ao meu lado

EXPRESSÕES ÚTEIS:

  1. "Things went from bad to worse." → As coisas foram de mal a pior.
  2. "I missed my flight." → Perdi meu voo.
  3. "I don't ever want it to stop." → Não quero que isso termine jamais.
  4. "You came along." → Você apareceu.

MÚSICA 03 — "Whenever I Travel Around the World"

Tema: Compras em viagem, barganha, dinheiro
Estilo: Pop alegre

TRECHO PRINCIPAL:

I go to the bank at a quarter to ten.
I pick up my cash from the ATM.
Here at the store it won't be too hard
to take out a check or a credit card.

The bank has a good rate of exchange
and everything here is in my price range.
The easiest part of this bargain hunt
is that I can afford anything I want.

Whenever I travel around the world
I spend my money for two —
Shopping for souvenirs helps me to be near you.

I try to decide how much I should pay
for the beautiful things I see on display.
To get a great deal I can beat the price —
It can't hurt to ask for a better price.

VOCABULÁRIO DA MÚSICA:

  • ATM = caixa eletrônico
  • rate of exchange = taxa de câmbio
  • price range = faixa de preço
  • bargain hunt = caça a pechinchas
  • souvenir = lembrança / souvenir
  • on display = em exposição
  • beat the price = superar o preço / conseguir mais barato
  • It can't hurt to ask = Não custa perguntar

FRASES-CHAVE:

  1. "It's in my price range." → Está na minha faixa de preço.
  2. "It can't hurt to ask." → Não custa perguntar.
  3. "I need to pick up some cash." → Preciso pegar dinheiro.
  4. "To get a great deal." → Para conseguir um bom negócio.

MÚSICA 04 — "Greetings and Small Talk"

Tema: Cumprimentos, conversa casual, conexão humana
Estilo: World music / Pop

TRECHO PRINCIPAL:

You look so familiar. Have we met before?
I don't think you're from around here.
It might have been two weeks ago, but I'm not sure.
Has it been a month or a year?

I have a funny feeling that I've met you twice.
That's what they call déjà vu.
You are saying something friendly, trying to be nice,
and now you're being friendly too.

One look. One word.
Is the friendliest sound that I've ever heard.
Thanks for your greetings. I'm glad this meeting occurred.
Greetings and small talk make the world go round.

Have you written any letters to your friends back home?
Have you had a chance to do that?
Have you spoken to your family on the telephone?
Have you taken time for a chat?

VOCABULÁRIO DA MÚSICA:

  • familiar = familiar / conhecido
  • déjà vu = déjà vu (sensação de já ter visto)
  • greetings = cumprimentos / saudações
  • small talk = conversa fiada / papo
  • make the world go round = faz o mundo girar
  • back home = lá em casa / no país de origem
  • have a chat = bater um papo

FRASES-CHAVE:

  1. "You look familiar." → Você parece familiar / Você tem uma cara conhecida.
  2. "Have we met before?" → Já nos conhecemos antes?
  3. "I have a funny feeling." → Tenho uma sensação estranha.
  4. "Greetings and small talk make the world go round." → Cumprimentos e papo fazem o mundo girar.
  5. "Have you had a chance to ___?" → Você teve chance de ___?

MÚSICA 05 — "The Colors of Love"

Tema: Emoções, perspectiva, felicidade
Estilo: Pop inspiracional

TRECHO PRINCIPAL:

Are you sick and tired of working hard day and night?
Do you like to look at the world in shades of black and white?
Your life can still be everything you were dreaming of —
Just take a look around you and see all the colors of love.

You wake up every morning and go through the same old grind.
You don't know how the light of the window could be so unkind.
If blue is the color that you choose when the road is rough,
You know you really need to believe in the colors of love.

The colors of love are as beautiful as a rainbow.
The colors of love shine on everyone in the world.

Our negative thoughts and emotions, painful to express,
Are just tiny drops in the ocean of happiness.
And these are the feelings you must learn to rise above.
Your whole life is a picture you paint with the colors of love.

VOCABULÁRIO DA MÚSICA:

  • sick and tired of = cansado de / farto de
  • shades of black and white = tons de preto e branco (sem cor / sem alegria)
  • the same old grind = a mesma rotina de sempre
  • unkind = cruel / duro
  • rough = difícil / áspero
  • tiny drops = gotinhas / pequenas gotas
  • rise above = superar / se elevar acima de

FRASES-CHAVE:

  1. "I'm sick and tired of ___." → Estou cansado de ___.
  2. "Go through the same old grind." → Passar pela mesma rotina de sempre.
  3. "Rise above it." → Supere isso / Eleve-se acima disso.
  4. "Your whole life is a picture you paint." → Toda a sua vida é um quadro que você pinta.

MÓDULO 3 — ENTREVISTAS COM NATIVOS

O que pessoas reais disseram sobre temas cotidianos

ENTREVISTA 01 — Música

Pergunta: "What kinds of music do you like? When do you usually listen to music?"

NATALIE disse:

I like classic rock. I like to see what's new.
I listen to music whenever I'm waking up in the morning and getting ready,
and also whenever I'm getting ready to go out in the evenings.
I always listen to music.
So I listen at least twice a day — in my office or in the car.
I go to classical music concerts and operas sometimes.

MAURO disse:

I like rock and roll. I like American music, as a matter of fact.
I don't own very many CDs, but my husband owns lots of CDs,
so I listen to his instead.
We have a few hundred. Wow, that's a lot!

VOCABULÁRIO:

  • classic rock = rock clássico
  • getting ready = se arrumando
  • as a matter of fact = na verdade / de fato
  • own = possuir / ter

FRASES ÚTEIS:

  1. "I listen to music whenever I'm ___." → Ouço música sempre que estou ___.
  2. "At least twice a day." → Pelo menos duas vezes por dia.
  3. "As a matter of fact..." → Na verdade... / De fato...
  4. "I don't own very many ___." → Não tenho muitos/as ___.

ENTREVISTA 02 — Família e diferenças entre irmãos

Pergunta: "How would you compare yourself with your sister? How are you alike and different?"

DEEPTI disse:

Well, we do look alike, but apart from that, we're very different.
She likes the arts, and I'm more interested in sport.
My sister is much better with money than I am.
She can save, whereas I like to spend.

ANGELIQUE disse:

Me and my brother are quite different.
I'm much more talkative, and he's much more shy.
But other than that, I mean, we grew up in the same house,
so we love the same food and listen to the same music pretty much,
and we like the same movies.

VOCABULÁRIO:

  • look alike = parecer-se / ter aparência similar
  • apart from that = além disso / fora isso
  • whereas = enquanto que / ao passo que
  • talkative = falante / comunicativo
  • shy = tímido
  • grew up = crescemos

FRASES ÚTEIS:

  1. "We look alike but we're very different." → Nos parecemos mas somos muito diferentes.
  2. "Apart from that..." → Além disso...
  3. "Whereas I like to ___." → Enquanto que eu gosto de ___.
  4. "We grew up in the same house." → Crescemos na mesma casa.

ENTREVISTA 03 — Exercício e saúde

Pergunta: "Are you an exercise fan? What do you do to stay in shape?"

UMA ENTREVISTADA disse:

Yes, I love to run. I run in the morning before work
and on Saturdays and Sundays along the river and through the park.

MARTIN disse:

Not really. So would you consider yourself a couch potato?
Well, I do go to the park and meet people in my age group.
They're 60, 70, 80 years old. We walk or run for about 3 and a half miles.
I go to the pool and walk in the water three days a week.

RITA disse:

I hate to exercise! Do you have a routine?
Yes, I do tai chi about once a week.
Do you feel exercise is important?
Yes, I think it's important — but not enough to do it more than once a week.

VOCABULÁRIO:

  • couch potato = pessoa sedentária / que fica no sofá
  • age group = faixa etária
  • stay in shape = ficar em forma / manter a forma
  • routine = rotina
  • tai chi = tai chi (prática chinesa)

FRASES ÚTEIS:

  1. "I run in the morning before work." → Corro de manhã antes do trabalho.
  2. "Would you consider yourself a couch potato?" → Você se considera sedentário?
  3. "I think it's important but not enough to do it more." → Acho importante mas não o suficiente para fazer mais.
  4. "I try to eat healthy foods — I don't always succeed." → Tento comer saudável — nem sempre consigo.

ENTREVISTA 04 — Viagem de avião

Pergunta: "Do you fly frequently? Have you had any problems with delayed or cancelled flights?"

CHRISTIANE disse:

Yes, I travel a lot with my job, so I'm always on an airplane.
I always want to sit at the aisle so I can stretch my legs.
I prefer to sit in the back of the plane at a window seat.
I always get a window seat — I like to sleep and I need something to lean against.

Sobre a pior experiência:

When I had to fly from Austria to America, I got stuck in London Airport
and had to wait 10 hours for a flight that got postponed, then cancelled.
All the stores were closed. All we could do was sleep on benches and on the floor
and try to find food that was not very good.
It was not a good experience. That sounds awful!
Yes, it was awful.

VOCABULÁRIO:

  • aisle seat = assento do corredor
  • window seat = assento da janela
  • stretch my legs = esticar as pernas
  • got stuck = ficou preso
  • postponed = adiado
  • benches = bancos
  • delayed = atrasado

FRASES ÚTEIS:

  1. "I always want to sit at the aisle." → Sempre quero sentar no corredor.
  2. "I got stuck at the airport." → Fiquei preso no aeroporto.
  3. "The flight was postponed, then cancelled." → O voo foi adiado e depois cancelado.
  4. "That sounds awful!" → Isso soa horrível!

MÓDULO 4 — TOP 50 FRASES DO VÍDEO

As mais úteis, naturais e frequentes — para usar imediatamente

01. "I'd like you to meet ___." → Quero que você conheça ___.
02. "Please, call me ___." → Por favor, me chame de ___.
03. "That's not my style." → Não é meu estilo.
04. "Sounds good!" → Parece bom!
05. "That's way past my bedtime!" → Isso é muito tarde pra mim!
06. "I'm looking for ___." → Estou procurando ___.
07. "Go straight two blocks." → Siga em frente dois quarteirões.
08. "Turn left at the corner." → Vire à esquerda na esquina.
09. "It's right there." → É bem ali.
10. "He's got a wife and two kids." → Ele tem esposa e dois filhos.
11. "Calm down. You're doing fine." → Calma. Você está indo bem.
12. "How much do you want for it?" → Quanto você quer por isso?
13. "I could go as low as ___." → Posso baixar até ___.
14. "It's a deal!" → Fechado!
15. "Not a dollar more." → Nem um centavo a mais.
16. "Can we get the check, please?" → Pode trazer a conta?
17. "Was there a problem with the service?" → Teve algum problema com o serviço?
18. "Never mind." → Deixa pra lá.
19. "Shall we go?" → Vamos?
20. "What do you think of ___?" → O que você acha de ___?
21. "I like them both the same." → Gosto dos dois igualmente.
22. "Who asked you anyway?" → Quem perguntou pra você?
23. "This is driving me crazy!" → Isso está me deixando louco!
24. "Stay away!" → Fique longe!
25. "Silly me!" → Que bobagem minha!
26. "I'm in the mood for ___." → Estou com vontade de ___.
27. "Could I order ___ without ___?" → Posso pedir ___ sem ___?
28. "What does it come with?" → O que vem junto?
29. "Just water, please." → Só água, por favor.
30. "I'll bet ___." → Aposto que ___.
31. "I'm seeing her tonight." → Vou encontrá-la esta noite.
32. "Is it an express ___?" → É um(a) ___ expresso/a?
33. "There are no cars on the island." → Não há carros na ilha.
34. "The printer won't work." → A impressora não está funcionando.
35. "My laptop crashed." → Meu laptop travou.
36. "Don't open the attachment." → Não abra o anexo.
37. "I'm down in the dumps." → Estou pra baixo.
38. "I can't put my finger on it." → Não consigo identificar.
39. "Works every time!" → Funciona sempre!
40. "I'm fascinated by it." → Estou fascinado com isso.
41. "I'm not so crazy about that." → Não sou muito fã disso.
42. "You have talent!" → Você tem talento!
43. "I'm getting in shape." → Estou ficando em forma.
44. "Exercise later. Work now." → Exercite depois. Trabalhe agora.
45. "Which do you like better?" → Qual você prefere?
46. "___ it is!" → Decidido: ___!
47. "How are we ever going to agree?" → Como vamos chegar a um acordo?
48. "Sounds okay to me." → Parece bom pra mim.
49. "We did it!" → Conseguimos!
50. "Everything will be all right." → Tudo vai ficar bem.

MÓDULO 5 — ROLE-PLAY: PRATIQUE AS CENAS

10 situações para você praticar como se estivesse no vídeo

ROLE-PLAY 01 — Apresentando alguém

Situação: Você está no escritório e precisa apresentar um novo colega para a equipe.

Sua vez:

Você: "_____, I'd like you to meet _____. He/She is our new _____."
Outros: "It's very nice to meet you!"
Você: "___ is from _____."

Pratique com: apresentar amigos, familiares, colegas.

ROLE-PLAY 02 — Pedindo direções

Situação: Você está perdido e precisa encontrar um lugar.

Você pergunta:

"Excuse me, I'm looking for _____. Could you help me?"

Eles respondem:

"Sure! Go straight two blocks, turn left, and it's on your right."

Você confirma:

"So I go straight, turn left, and it's on my right? Thank you!"

ROLE-PLAY 03 — No restaurante

Situação: Você quer fazer um pedido com modificações.

Waiter: "Are you ready to order?"
Você: "I'm in the mood for the chicken, but could I order it without the sauce?"
Waiter: "Sure. What would you like instead?"
Você: "Could I have grilled vegetables instead?"
Waiter: "Of course. Anything to drink?"
Você: "Just water, please."

ROLE-PLAY 04 — Barganhando

Situação: Você quer comprar algo mas o preço é alto.

Vendedor: "This is $100."
Você: "That's more than I want to pay. Could you do $80?"
Vendedor: "I could go as low as $90."
Você: "How about $85?"
Vendedor: "$87. That's my final offer."
Você: "It's a deal!"

ROLE-PLAY 05 — Falando sobre planos de fim de semana

Situação: Seus amigos perguntam o que você quer fazer.

Amigo: "Do you guys want to go out this weekend?"
Você A: "A rock concert sounds good to me."
Você B: "Not my style. I'd love to see a movie."
Você C: "How about a play?"
Amigo: "There's a concert Saturday at 8pm. Sounds good?"
Você: "Sounds great! I can't wait!"

SISTEMA 12 — ROTINA DA NOITE

ESTRUTURA — 10 TEMAS

  1. Chegada em casa — lavar mãos, trocar roupa, beber, comer
  2. Relaxamento — TV, música, exercício, silêncio
  3. Estudos — lição de casa, computador, inglês, revisão
  4. Família — ajudar, jogar, conversar, compartilhar
  5. Refeição noturna — jantar, cozinhar, lavar louça
  6. Ao ar livre — caminhada, vizinhos, pôr do sol, estrelas
  7. Organização — quartos, livros, agenda, planejamento
  8. Reflexão — diário, metas, meditação, gratidão
  9. Preparação para amanhã — roupas, bolsa, alarme, planos
  10. Dormir — higiene, pijama, leitura, descanso

SISTEMA 18 — HOW WAS YOUR DAY? 30 RESPOSTAS AUTÊNTICAS

ESTRUTURA — 5 CATEGORIAS DE HUMOR/SENTIMENTO

CategoriaTomN°
😊 Bom / PositivoFeliz, produtivo, tranquilo8
😐 NeutroNem bom nem ruim — o dia foi o dia5
😓 Ocupado / CansativoCorreria, tarefas, sem fôlego10
📉 Poderia ter sido melhorFrustração leve, honesto4
😅 Humorístico / DramáticoFaz rir, exagero saudável3

CONTEÚDO PRINCIPAL — 30 RESPOSTAS

😊 CATEGORIA 1 — BOM / POSITIVO (8 respostas)

#RespostaSignificadoNuance
1I got a lot done today.Fui muito produtivoMuito otimista e positivo — implica satisfação com o dia
2I felt really on top of it today.Me senti organizado e no controle"On top of it" = estar por cima, tudo sob controle, sem erros
3I was in a really good mood all day.Fiquei de bom humor o dia todoPode não ter motivo específico — basta estar feliz
4It went by really fast.O dia passou rápidoImplica que estava ocupada mas de forma boa — o tempo voa quando você está engajado
5Long day but a good one.Dia longo mas bomReconhece o esforço mas termina no positivo — tom equilibrado e maduro
6It was challenging but worth it.Foi desafiador mas valeuIdeal quando o dia foi difícil mas você se sente orgulhoso
7It flew by before I knew it.Passou voando — não vi a hora passarVariante mais poética de "it went by fast"
8I finally checked a few things off my list.Finalmente fiz o que precisava fazerImplica que essas coisas estavam pendentes há um tempo — sensação de alívio

😐 CATEGORIA 2 — NEUTRO (5 respostas)

#RespostaSignificadoNuance
9It was pretty uneventful.Foi um dia normal/sem novidades"Pretty" = intensificador suave — "uneventful" = sem eventos notáveis. Não é ruim!
10Not too bad, actually.Não foi ruim, na verdade foi até bomO "actually" é chave — significa que foi melhor do que parece. Levemente positivo.
11Same old, same old.Tudo igual, mesma rotina de sempreNeutro sem reclamação — reconhece a repetição sem estar irritado por isso
12I can't complain.Não tenho do que reclamarEducado, positivo, humilde. Tudo estava bem o suficiente.
13It started out rough but it got better.Começou ruim mas melhorouColoca um spin positivo no final — "rough" = difícil/desconfortável

😓 CATEGORIA 3 — OCUPADO / CANSATIVO (10 respostas)

#RespostaSignificadoNuance
14I was putting out fires all day.Fiquei resolvendo problemas o dia todo"Put out fires" = apagar incêndios (metáfora) — muito usado no ambiente de trabalho americano
15I was juggling a bunch of different things.Fiquei malabarando várias coisas ao mesmo tempo"Juggling" = malabarismo — metáfora visual de manter muitas coisas no ar
16It felt like one thing after another.Foi um problema atrás do outroTom mais negativo — sensação de que nunca acabava
17I barely had time to breathe.Mal tive tempo de respirarMuito dramático e expressivo — dia absolutamente sem pausa
18I spent most of my day running errands.Passei a maior parte do dia fazendo tarefas externas"Errands" = tarefas fora de casa: mercado, banco, correio, consultas
19I was chasing my kids around all day.Fiquei correndo atrás das crianças o dia todoHumorístico — dito por pais com filhos pequenos e ativos
20It was one of those non-stop days.Foi um daqueles dias sem pausa"Non-stop" = sem parar. Às vezes dito apenas: "It was non-stop."
21It drained my energy.Me drenou a energiaPode ser "it drained me" — dia estressante ou emocionalmente pesado
22Honestly, it was kind of exhausting.Pra ser honesto, foi meio cansativoO "kind of" suaviza — não está reclamando excessivamente, só sendo honesto
23It was busier than I expected.Foi mais corrido do que eu esperavaNeutro — simplesmente não esperava essa quantidade de coisas

📉 CATEGORIA 4 — PODERIA TER SIDO MELHOR (4 respostas)

#RespostaSignificadoNuance
24I didn't get as much done as I hoped.Não consegui fazer tudo que queriaAdmite improdutividade sem drama — honesto e maduro
25I was just trying to stay on top of everything.Estava só tentando manter tudo organizadoImplica que estava difícil de controlar, mas você estava tentando
26I needed a break by the end of it.Precisava de uma pausa no final do diaDescreve como você se sentiu no final — válido para dias longos mas não necessariamente ruins
27I had a few detours.Tive alguns desvios / aconteceram coisas inesperadas"Detour" = desvio de rota. Pode ser positivo (algo divertido e inesperado) ou neutro

😅 CATEGORIA 5 — HUMORÍSTICO / DRAMÁTICO (3 respostas)

#RespostaSignificadoNuance
28I survived.Sobrevivi.Humor — usado quando o dia foi muito difícil. Tom de alívio cômico.
29I'm just glad it's over.Fico feliz que acabou.Humor + drama — indica que o dia foi difícil, mas você pode sorrir agora que terminou.
30It was a bit stressful.Foi um pouco estressanteMenos humorístico, mas honesto. O "a bit" suaviza a reclamação.

VOCABULÁRIO CHAVE — EXPRESSÕES EXTRAÍDAS

InglêsPortuguêsNota
uneventfulsem eventos / sem novidades"an uneventful day" = dia normal, sem nada de especial
pretty (intensifier)bastante / meiouso coloquial: "pretty good" = bem bom; não é sobre beleza aqui
actuallyna verdadeusado para corrigir uma expectativa ou surpreender — não é "atualmente"!
put out firesapagar incêndios / resolver crisesmetáfora do ambiente de trabalho americano
jugglemalabarismo / fazer várias coisas ao mesmo tempo"juggling tasks" = tentando dar conta de tudo
errandsrecados / tarefas do dia a dia fora de casamercado, banco, correio, farmácia — tudo é "errand"
non-stopsem parar / incessante"It was non-stop" = não parei um segundo
draindrenar / esgotar energia"it drained me" = me deixou sem energia
check off (a list)riscar / marcar como feito"check things off my list" = marcar na lista de afazeres
roughdifícil / turbulento"a rough start" = começo difícil; "rough day" = dia ruim
on top of it / on top of everythingpor cima / no controle"I felt on top of it" = senti que controlava tudo
detourdesvio / surpresa no percursoliteral: desvio de rota. Figurativo: coisa inesperada no dia
stay on top ofmanter o controle de"trying to stay on top of everything" = tentando não perder controle
worth itvaleu a pena"it was worth it" = valeu o esforço
flew bypassou voando"it flew by" = o tempo passou rápido

ARMADILHAS PARA BRASILEIROS

ArmadilhaErro BRCorreto
"Actually""Atualmente""Na verdade" — "actually" NUNCA significa "currently/nowadays"
"Pretty""Bonito"Intensificador coloquial: "pretty good" = bem bom
"Rough"DesconhecidaDifícil / turbulento: "rough day", "rough start"
"Errands"Sem equivalente diretoTarefas cotidianas fora de casa (mercado, banco, etc.)
"Kind of""Tipo de"Suavizador: "kind of exhausting" = meio cansativo
"Drain"Ralo do banheiroDrenar energia: "it drained me" = me esgotou

What is inside the box?A gift is inside the box.
Where is my phone charger?Your charger is on the desk.
Where should I put this?You should put it on the shelf.
Have you seen my keys?No, I haven't seen them.
Where were the keys found?They were found under the sofa.
Have you lost your keys?Yes, I have lost them.
Where does the cat sleep?The cat sleeps on the sofa.
Is the water safe to drink?Yes, the water is safe to drink.
Does this path lead home?Yes, this path leads home.

PADRÕES GRAMATICAIS DESTACADOS

PadrãoExemplos
Yes/No questionsIs he married? / Are you happy? / Does this bus go to...?
Wh- questionsWho is your hero? / What is your name? / Where can I find...?
How long...?How long does the flight take? / How long have you studied?
How often...?How often do you brush teeth? / How often do you change sheets?
Have you ever...?Have you tried sushi? / Have you lost your keys? / Have you seen my keys?
Could you...?Could you send the email? / Could we have the bill?
Should I...?Should I call the doctor? / Should we take an umbrella?
Will...?Will it be sunny? / Will he join us later? / When will you be back?
Why...?Why are you angry? / Why did you sell your bike? / Why is she crying?
Whose...?Whose idea was this? / Whose jacket is hanging there?

SISTEMA 20 — CONVERSAS REAIS: INFÂNCIA, AMIZADE E VIDA LÁ FORA

ESTRUTURA — 4 BLOCOS TEMÁTICOS

#BlocoConteúdo
1Vocabulário de Infância10 palavras/expressões com exemplos reais
2Gramática: Used ToEstrutura completa para falar do passado
3Aprendendo Idiomas: Vocabulário RealExpressões sobre aprendizado, medo, prática
4Vida e Diferenças CulturaisEUA vs. Espanha — expressões contextuais

CONTEÚDO PRINCIPAL

BLOCO 1 — VOCABULÁRIO DE INFÂNCIA

Palavra/ExpressãoDefiniçãoExemplo Real do Episódio
grow upCrescer / se criar (como criança)"I grew up in a small town." / "Where did you grow up?"
best friendMelhor amigo — o mais próximo, a quem você conta tudo"My best friend's name was Sarah. We are still best friends today."
playgroundParquinho / área de recreação na escola"We used to play on the playground every break."
pocket moneyMesada — pequena quantia que os pais dão às crianças"I used to save my pocket money for months to buy a toy."
piggy bankCofrinho (normalmente em forma de porquinho)"I had a little ceramic pig, a piggy bank, and I used to put my coins in it."
school tripExcursão escolar"I used to love school trips because you didn't have lessons."
sports dayDia de esportes na escola — competições com pais assistindo"Every year our school had a sports day. Parents came, teachers came, everyone watched."
puddlePoça d'água"Not a big river — more like a wide puddle, really." (usado de forma humorística)
pocket moneyMesada infantil"I used to spend all my pocket money on sweets on Fridays."
tuck shopCantina / lojinha de guloseimas"We had a tuck shop, a little window where you could buy sweets during break."

BLOCO 2 — GRAMÁTICA: USED TO

O que é:
"Used to" descreve hábitos ou situações regulares no passado que não acontecem mais. É essencial para falar sobre a infância — o que você COSTUMAVA fazer.

Estrutura:

TipoFórmulaExemplo
Afirmativosubject + used to + base verbI used to eat cereal for dinner.
Negativosubject + didn't use to + base verbI didn't use to like vegetables.
PerguntaDid + subject + use to + base verb?Did you use to play outside?

Exemplos reais do episódio:

  • "I used to go there every weekend with my dad."
  • "I used to ride my pink bicycle every day after school."
  • "We used to have sleepovers every Friday."
  • "I used to stay up all night talking and laughing."
  • "I used to spend all my pocket money on sweets."
  • "When I was a kid, I used to eat cereal for dinner."
  • "I used to love school trips because there were no lessons."

Cuidado — "used to" vs "get used to":

  • "I used to play outside" → hábito do passado (não faço mais)
  • "I got used to the noise" → me acostumei com (passei a aceitar/tolerar)
  • São expressões completamente diferentes!

Frases modelo para falar de si mesmo:

  • "When I was a child, I used to ___."
  • "I didn't use to like ___, but now I love it."
  • "My best friend and I used to ___ every weekend."
  • "I used to live in ___ before I moved to ___."

BLOCO 3 — APRENDER IDIOMAS: VOCABULÁRIO REAL

Extraído da conversa entre Maria e Kieran (English Cozy Chat) sobre aprender espanhol e inglês.

ExpressãoSignificadoContexto real
obstacleobstáculo — algo difícil de superar"The biggest obstacle when learning a language is the fear of speaking."
preventimpedir — bloquear algo de acontecer"It was my own fear that prevented [me from speaking]."
mess uperrar / estragar / se atrapalhar"I was scared of messing up." / "When I forget I'm speaking the language, that's when I speak the best."
challenge yourselfse desafiar"Challenge yourself without judgment."
without judgmentsem julgamento"Challenge yourself without judgment." — conselho do marido de Kieran
from scratchdo zero / sem preparação anterior"You have to cook everything from scratch." (contexto: comida)
one thing led to anotheruma coisa levou a outra"I started taking classes and one thing led to another."
rewardinggratificante / recompensador"That's also got to be really rewarding." (sobre fazer algo com as mãos)
language exchangetroca de idiomas"I found someone who wanted to learn English and I wanted to learn Spanish — we would meet and help each other."
mannerismsmaneirismos / gestos / jeito de falar"He speaks with the Spanish mannerisms — ways of saying things you only learn from watching a native speaker."
absorbabsorver / assimilar"When your brain is having fun, it learns better. It's much easier for it to absorb information."
roller coastermontanha-russa"Learning a language — there are good days and bad days and you're embarrassed and happy. It's a roller coaster."
tutorprofessor particular"I got a tutor and was learning Spanish."
fluentfluente"Kieran is fluent in Spanish."

BLOCO 4 — VIDA E DIFERENÇAS CULTURAIS (EUA vs. ESPANHA)

ExpressãoSignificadoExemplo
off the top of my headde primeira / sem pensar muito"Off the top of my head, one thing that surprised me was..."
convenientconveniente / prático / fácil de acessar"Life in Spain is not as convenient as the US."
pre-madepronto / pré-preparado"It's hard to find good pre-made items."
slow downdesacelerar / ir mais devagar"Living here forces you to slow down a lot more."
thoughtfulatencioso / cuidadoso com os outros"Maria is always so thoughtful and cares about everyone around her."
gratefulgrato / agradecido"I'm really, really grateful to have her here."
inexpensivebarato / econômico (mais educado que "cheap")"Trader Joe's has really inexpensive, good products."
communitycomunidade"Maybe there's someone in your community you could reach out to."
reach outentrar em contato / buscar alguém"Reach out to talk to someone in English."
don't get hard on yourselfnão se culpe / não seja duro consigo mesmo"Be kind to yourself and keep going."

ARMADILHAS PARA BRASILEIROS

ExpressãoO BR pensaA verdade
used to"usado para"Hábito do passado: "costumava fazer"
get used tomesma coisa que "used to"São diferentes! "get used to" = se acostumar com algo
convenient"conveniente" (aprovado, adequado)Prático / fácil de usar / de acessar — não exatamente "aprovado"
grateful"grato"Correto! Mas "thankful" e "grateful" são sinônimos naturais
obstacle"obstáculo"Correto! Mas em inglês falado soa mais natural que no português
prevent"prevenir"Impedir — não apenas "prevenir" (que pode ser "prevent" ou "avoid")
reward / rewarding"recompensa"Correto — mas "rewarding" (adj.) = gratificante, que compensa

SISTEMA 26 — DIÁLOGOS DO DIA A DIA: CONVERSAS REAIS EM 12 SITUAÇÕES

AS 12 SITUAÇÕES — DIÁLOGOS SELECIONADOS

SITUAÇÃO 1 — Saudações e Pequena Conversa (Greetings & Small Talk)

Diálogo A:
> A: Good morning!
> B: Good morning to you too. Do you think it will rain today?
> A: Yeah, maybe. It's hard to tell.
> B: I hope not — I'm going to the beach this afternoon.
> A: Maybe you should check the weather forecast first.
> B: Good idea. I think I will. Well, I hope you have a good afternoon.
> A: You too.

Diálogo B:
> A: Hello, Bill! How are you doing?
> B: Not bad — work is going well.
> A: Oh, is it? That's good to hear. What about you?
> B: I'm doing okay, although my car is in the shop.
> A: Oh really? That's too bad.

Diálogo C:
> A: What's up, Andrew?
> B: Not much. Not much at all. Are you hungry?
> A: A little. What are you thinking?
> B: I was thinking we could grab a bite somewhere.
> A: Sounds good to me.

Expressões-chave:

  • It's hard to tell — difícil dizer, não dá para saber
  • That's good to hear — que bom ouvir isso
  • Although — embora (adicionar ressalva a algo positivo)
  • That's too bad — que pena
  • What's up? — E aí? O que há?
  • Not much — Nada demais
  • Grab a bite — comer alguma coisa rapidamente
  • Sounds good to me — me parece bem / topa

SITUAÇÃO 2 — Ligações Telefônicas (Making Phone Calls)

Diálogo A — Ligação pessoal:
> A: Hello, Jane? This is Dad.
> B: Oh hi, Dad! What are you doing?
> A: I just thought I'd call to see how you're doing.
> B: I'm doing okay, but I can't talk long right now.
> A: I'm sorry — is this not a good time?
> B: I'm just about to go out with some friends to dinner.
> A: It's good to hear you're making friends. When is it a good time to call back?
> B: Just call me about this time tomorrow. I should be here.
> A: Okay, I'll do that. Have fun tonight!
> B: I will. It was good to hear from you. Love you, Dad.
> A: Love you too. Bye.

Diálogo B — Pedido de pizza:
> A: Thank you for calling Joe's Pizza. How may I help you?
> B: Yes, can I place an order for delivery?
> A: Yes, you may. Go right ahead.
> B: I'd like two medium pizzas, both with olives and ham.
> A: Is that all?
> B: I'd also like a 2-liter bottle of Coke.
> A: Would you like any breadsticks?
> B: Sure, that'll be fine.
> A: Your total comes to $17.80. Can I have your address?
> B: 1480 Poplar Drive.
> A: How long will it take?
> B: It should be there within 45 minutes.
> A: Thanks.

Diálogo C — Ligar para o médico:
> A: Hello, is this Dr. Cooper's office?
> B: Yes, it is. What can I do for you?
> A: My dog needs some shots. We can do that here.
> B: What kind of dog do you have?
> A: He's a German Shepherd. He's about a year old.
> B: What day would you like to come in?
> A: Sometime early next week would be best for me.
> B: How about next Tuesday morning?
> A: That would be fine.

Expressões-chave:

  • I just thought I'd call — pensei em ligar (tom casual e gentil)
  • Is this not a good time? — não é uma boa hora? (verificar disponibilidade)
  • It was good to hear from you — foi bom ouvir de você / foi bom falar com você
  • Thank you for calling [nome] — abertura padrão de atendimento telefônico
  • How may I help you? — Como posso ajudar? (forma educada)
  • Go right ahead — pode falar / pode continuar
  • Is that all? — é só isso?
  • Your total comes to... — seu total é...
  • How about [dia/hora]? — que tal [dia/hora]?

SITUAÇÃO 3 — Convites e Planos (Invitations & Making Plans)

Diálogo A — Convite para jantar:
> A: I just called to see if you wanted to come over for dinner this Saturday night.
> B: Really? I'd love to! What's the reason?
> A: I'm just having a few students over for dinner since it's the end of the year.
> B: What a great idea!
> A: It's just to celebrate the end of the school year. I do this every year.
> B: Great. Should I bring anything?
> A: No, just bring yourself.
> B: Okay, what time should I be there?
> A: Come here around 7:00. Do you know how to get here?
> B: I think so — it's just north of the school, right?
> A: Yes, that's right. I'll see you then.

Diálogo B — Combinando um programa:
> A: Are you free this weekend?
> B: I think so — what did you have in mind?
> A: I was thinking we could go hiking.
> B: Sounds fun! What time were you thinking?
> A: Maybe early morning, around 8:00?
> B: That works for me. Do you want to drive, or should I?
> A: I can drive. I'll pick you up.
> B: Perfect. See you Saturday!

Diálogo C — Adiando planos:
> A: Hey, are we still on for tonight?
> B: Actually, something came up. Could we reschedule?
> A: Of course! No problem. How about next week?
> B: Next week works better. I'm sorry about this.
> A: Don't worry about it. It happens.

Expressões-chave:

  • come over — vir à minha casa / visitar
  • I'd love to! — adoraria! (aceitar convite com entusiasmo)
  • Should I bring anything? — devo trazer alguma coisa?
  • Just bring yourself — não precisa trazer nada (expressão gentil)
  • What did you have in mind? — o que você tinha em mente?
  • That works for me — funciona para mim / pode ser
  • Are we still on for...? — ainda estamos combinados para...?
  • Something came up — surgiu algo / aconteceu um imprevisto
  • Could we reschedule? — podemos remarcar?
  • Don't worry about it — não tem problema / deixa para lá

SITUAÇÃO 4 — Pedidos de Desculpas (Apologies)

Diálogo A:
> A: I'm really sorry I'm late. The traffic was terrible.
> B: It's okay. It happens.
> A: I should have left earlier. I apologize.
> B: Don't apologize — you're here now. That's what matters.

Diálogo B:
> A: I owe you an apology.
> B: What for?
> A: I forgot about our meeting yesterday. I completely lost track of time.
> B: I was waiting for you for 20 minutes.
> A: I know. I feel terrible about it. It won't happen again.
> B: I appreciate that. Just give me a heads-up next time if something comes up.
> A: Absolutely. Thanks for understanding.

Expressões-chave:

  • I should have [done X] — eu deveria ter feito X (arrependimento)
  • I owe you an apology — te devo um pedido de desculpas
  • I completely lost track of time — perdi a noção do tempo completamente
  • I feel terrible about it — me sinto péssimo com isso
  • It won't happen again — não vai acontecer de novo
  • Give me a heads-up — me avise com antecedência
  • Thanks for understanding — obrigado pela compreensão

SITUAÇÃO 5 — Gostos e Preferências (Likes, Dislikes & Opinions)

Diálogo A:
> A: Do you like hiking?
> B: I love it, actually. I try to go every weekend.
> A: Really? I've never tried it. What's it like?
> B: It's really peaceful. And the views are incredible.
> A: Maybe you should take me sometime.
> B: I'd be happy to!

Diálogo B:
> A: What kind of music do you listen to?
> B: Mostly jazz and classical. What about you?
> A: I'm more into pop and R&B, honestly.
> B: That's cool. We all have different tastes.
> A: I tried to get into jazz once, but I just couldn't.
> B: It grows on you. Give it some time.

Expressões-chave:

  • I love it, actually — na verdade, adoro (o "actually" suaviza uma resposta entusiástica)
  • What's it like? — como é? Como é a experiência?
  • Maybe you should take me sometime — talvez você devesse me levar um dia
  • I'm more into... — sou mais de... / prefiro... (gostos pessoais)
  • We all have different tastes — todo mundo tem gostos diferentes
  • It grows on you — você vai pegando gosto com o tempo

SITUAÇÃO 6 — Reclamações (Complaints)

Diálogo A — Reclamação de conta:
> A: Thank you for calling Bell Atlantic. How may I help you?
> B: Yeah, I've got a real problem here. My last phone bill was for $1,493.
> A: Is this amount incorrect?
> B: You bet it's incorrect! It says here I made nine calls to Shanghai.
> A: And you did not make those calls?
> B: I repair motorboats. Why would I call Shanghai?
> A: Wait just one moment, and I'll transfer you to a manager.
> B: Okay, good.

Diálogo B — Reclamação do clima:
> A: I hate this weather.
> B: I know what you mean. It's been raining for days.
> A: I was supposed to have a picnic this weekend.
> B: That's a bummer. Maybe you can reschedule.
> A: I hope so. I've been looking forward to it for weeks.

Expressões-chave:

  • I've got a real problem here — tenho um sério problema aqui
  • You bet it's incorrect — pode apostar que está errado (forma enfática de concordar)
  • I'll transfer you to a manager — vou te transferir para um gerente
  • That's a bummer — que chateação / que pena (informal)
  • I've been looking forward to it — estava ansioso por isso
  • I know what you mean — entendo o que você quer dizer / sei bem como é

SITUAÇÃO 7 — Concordar e Discordar (Agreement & Disagreement)

Diálogo A:
> A: I don't think social media is good for young people.
> B: I disagree completely. It helps them stay connected.
> A: But the constant comparison is damaging.
> B: I see your point, but it depends how you use it.
> A: Fair enough. Maybe it's more about balance.
> B: Exactly. That's what I think too.

Diálogo B:
> A: I think working from home is more productive.
> B: Do you? I actually find it harder to focus at home.
> A: Really? I'm way more productive without the office noise.
> B: I need the structure of being in an office, personally.
> A: That makes sense. We're all different.

Expressões-chave:

  • I disagree completely — discordo completamente
  • I see your point — entendo o que você está dizendo / vejo seu argumento
  • But it depends — mas depende (usado para qualificar opiniões)
  • Fair enough — justo / faz sentido (concessão parcial)
  • That makes sense — faz sentido
  • Personally — pessoalmente (para marcar que é uma opinião sua)
  • We're all different — somos todos diferentes (forma de encerrar uma discussão gentilmente)

SITUAÇÃO 8 — Elogios (Compliments)

Diálogo A:
> A: I love your jacket! Where did you get it?
> B: Thank you! I found it at a thrift store, actually.
> A: No way! It looks brand new.
> B: I know, right? I got lucky.

Diálogo B:
> A: You did a great job on that presentation.
> B: Oh, thanks. I was really nervous about it.
> A: You couldn't tell at all. You seemed very confident.
> B: That means a lot. I practiced for hours.
> A: Well, it paid off. Everyone was impressed.

Expressões-chave:

  • Where did you get it? — onde você comprou / achou?
  • No way! — Não acredito! (surpresa positiva)
  • You did a great job on... — você fez um ótimo trabalho em...
  • You couldn't tell at all — não dava para perceber / não deu para notar
  • That means a lot — isso significa muito para mim
  • It paid off — valeu a pena / compensou

SITUAÇÃO 9 — Estudos e Escola (Studies & College)

Diálogo A:
> A: How's your biology class going?
> B: It's interesting, but there's so much work.
> A: That's what I was told. I'm glad I picked chemistry this semester.
> B: Chemistry's not that simple either.
> A: I know, but I feel more comfortable with numbers.

Diálogo B:
> A: Are you ready for the history test tomorrow?
> B: Not really. There's so much to memorize.
> A: Let's test each other. We'll make it like a game show.
> B: That sounds fun. You go first.
> A: Okay. In what year did World War II end?
> B: 1945!
> A: Correct!

Diálogo C — Pedindo ajuda a um professor:
> A: Hello, Mr. Taylor. Can I ask you a favor?
> B: Sure, Ken. What do you need?
> A: There are some things in class I'm having trouble with. I wanted to set up a time to meet.
> B: When would you like to meet?
> A: Any afternoon this week, if possible.
> B: Friday afternoon works for me. Shall we meet at 4:00 in the student center?
> A: Yes, that sounds good. I'll see you then.

Expressões-chave:

  • How's [subject] class going? — como está indo a aula de [matéria]?
  • There's so much [work/to memorize] — tem tanta coisa para [fazer/memorizar]
  • Let's test each other — vamos nos testar mutuamente
  • Can I ask you a favor? — posso te pedir um favor?
  • I'm having trouble with... — estou tendo dificuldade com...
  • Set up a time to meet — marcar um horário para se encontrar
  • Shall we meet at...? — que tal nos encontrarmos às...? (forma formal de propor horário)

SITUAÇÃO 10 — Atividades Diárias (Daily Activities)

Diálogo A:
> A: Where are you going at this hour? It's almost midnight.
> B: I need to go to the store. I have a job interview tomorrow and I'm out of razor blades.
> A: I guess you don't want to make a bad impression.
> B: Exactly. To be honest, I hate shaving every day.
> A: I can't sympathize — I don't have to shave every day.
> B: Some guys don't. They're lucky.

Diálogo B:
> A: I'm tired of studying. Let's go do something fun.
> B: What do you want to do?
> A: Let's go play catch with a football.
> B: Good idea. It's nice weather for it — very crisp and cool.
> A: I'll grab the ball. Meet me outside in five minutes.

Expressões-chave:

  • At this hour — a esta hora (surpresa com o horário)
  • I'm out of [something] — estou sem [algo] / acabou meu estoque de
  • Make a bad impression — causar má impressão
  • I can't sympathize — não consigo ter empatia com isso / não sei como é
  • I'm tired of [doing something] — estou cansado de [fazer algo]
  • Let's go do something fun — vamos fazer algo divertido
  • Crisp — frescante e limpo (descrever clima frio mas agradável)
  • Meet me outside — me encontra lá fora

SITUAÇÃO 11 — Passado e Memórias (Talking About the Past)

Diálogo A:
> A: It's cold out today — it kind of reminds me of that trip we took with Mom and Dad to Canada.
> B: You mean the one we took when we were very young?
> A: Yes. You may have been too young to remember.
> B: Actually, I remember it pretty well. It was freezing.
> A: I remember Dad got lost trying to find the hotel.
> B: And Mom kept saying "I told you so."
> A: Ha! Classic.

Diálogo B:
> A: Remember when you borrowed Dad's car on Christmas?
> B: That's right! I almost forgot.
> A: You drove it into a mailbox.
> B: I don't know how I forgot — Dad was so upset.
> A: That was the last time he ever let you drive his car.
> B: Some things you never live down.

Expressões-chave:

  • It kind of reminds me of... — isso me lembra um pouco de...
  • You may have been too young to remember — você pode ter sido jovem demais para lembrar
  • Actually, I remember it pretty well — na verdade, lembro bem
  • Classic — clássico (reação a algo típico de uma pessoa)
  • Some things you never live down — tem coisa que você nunca vai conseguir esquecer / que persegue você
  • I almost forgot — quase esqueci
  • I told you so — eu te falei! / eu avisei!

SITUAÇÃO 12 — Futuro e Planos (Future Plans)

Diálogo A:
> A: I think we're going to save some extra money this year.
> B: Is that because of the tax cuts?
> A: That's right. Do you think we should spend that money or keep saving it?
> B: I think we should take a trip somewhere.
> A: That's not a bad idea. Where would you want to go?
> B: Somewhere warm. Maybe the Caribbean.
> A: I love that idea. Let's start planning.

Diálogo B:
> A: What are your plans for after graduation?
> B: I'm thinking about applying to medical school.
> A: That won't be easy. Good luck!
> B: Thanks. I know it's going to be a lot of work.
> A: Well, if anyone can do it, you can.
> B: I appreciate that. I need all the encouragement I can get.

Expressões-chave:

  • That's not a bad idea — não é uma má ideia (forma gentil de concordar)
  • Let's start planning — vamos começar a planejar
  • What are your plans for...? — quais são seus planos para...?
  • I'm thinking about [doing] — estou pensando em [fazer]
  • That won't be easy — não vai ser fácil
  • If anyone can do it, you can — se alguém é capaz, esse alguém é você (elogio de incentivo)
  • I need all the encouragement I can get — preciso de todo o incentivo que puder conseguir

EXPRESSÕES CONVERSACIONAIS ESSENCIAIS (ORGANIZADAS POR FUNÇÃO)

Para Responder com Entusiasmo

ExpressãoUso
I'd love to!aceitar convite com entusiasmo
Sounds great! / Sounds good to me!concordar com plano/ideia
That's a great idea!reagir positivamente a uma sugestão
No way!surpresa positiva

Para Concordar Parcialmente

ExpressãoUso
Fair enoughjusto, faz sentido
I see your pointentendo o argumento
That makes sensefaz sentido
I can see where you're coming fromentendo de onde você vem

Para Recusar Gentilmente

ExpressãoUso
I'm afraid I can'tme desculpe, não posso
Something came upsurgiu um imprevisto
Could we reschedule?podemos remarcar?
Maybe another timequem sabe outra vez

Para Verificar / Confirmar

ExpressãoUso
Is this a good time?agora é uma boa hora?
Are we still on for...?ainda estamos combinados para...?
Does that work for you?funciona para você?
Shall we say [hora]?que tal [hora]?

Para Encerrar uma Conversa

ExpressãoUso
It was good to hear from youfoi bom falar com você
I've got to run / I've got to gopreciso ir
Talk to you latera gente fala depois

Don't worry about itnão tem problema

Para Expressar Surpresa ou Empatia

That's a bummerque chateação (informal)

It happensacontece (consolando alguém)

Where can we pick up our luggage?Onde podemos pegar nossa bagagem?

BLOCO 6 — EMERGÊNCIAS

Frase em InglêsTradução / Uso
Help! I need assistance immediately.Socorro! Preciso de ajuda imediatamente.

Can you help me? I'm lost.Pode me ajudar? Estou perdido.
Is there a doctor here?Há algum médico aqui?
I need a police officer.Preciso de um policial.
Fire! Get out quickly!Fogo! Saiam rápido!

BLOCO 7 — CONVERSAS DIFÍCEIS

Frase em InglêsTradução / Uso
I'm sorry for any misunderstanding. Can we discuss this further?Me desculpe por qualquer mal-entendido. Podemos discutir mais?
I appreciate your perspective, but I see things differently.Aprecio sua perspectiva, mas vejo as coisas de forma diferente.
Could you please clarify what you mean by that?Você poderia esclarecer o que quis dizer com isso?
I'm not comfortable discussing this right now. Can we talk about it later?Não me sinto confortável em discutir isso agora. Podemos falar depois?
I didn't mean to offend you. My apologies if I did.Não quis ofender você. Me desculpe se ofendi.
I understand this is a sensitive topic. Let's approach it with care.Entendo que este é um assunto sensível. Vamos abordá-lo com cuidado.
I need a moment to process this. Can we pause for a second?Preciso de um momento para processar isso. Podemos pausar?
I'm not sure I agree, but I'm willing to listen to your point of view.Não tenho certeza se concordo, mas estou disposto a ouvir seu ponto de vista.
That's an interesting point. I hadn't considered it that way before.É um ponto interessante. Não tinha considerado dessa forma antes.
I'm sorry, but I have to disagree with you on that.Me desculpe, mas preciso discordar de você nisso.
Could we find a compromise that works for both of us?Poderíamos encontrar um acordo que funcione para nós dois?
It seems there's been a misunderstanding. Let's try to clear it up.Parece que houve um mal-entendido. Vamos tentar esclarecê-lo.
I feel a bit out of my depth here. Can you explain further?Me sinto um pouco perdido aqui. Pode explicar mais?
Let's agree to disagree on this one.Vamos concordar em discordar neste ponto.
I think we're getting off track. Let's refocus on the main issue.Acho que estamos saindo do assunto. Vamos focar na questão principal.

BLOCO 8 — PHRASAL VERBS EM CONTEXTO

Os phrasal verbs mais úteis, extraídos do episódio "1200 Frases", organizados por grupo temático:

Grupo A: Começar / Terminar / Continuar

Phrasal VerbSignificadoExemplo real

go oncontinuar / prosseguir"Please go on and tell me the rest of the story."
keep oncontinuar fazendo"Keep on practicing and you'll improve."
give updesistir"Don't give up on your dreams, keep pursuing them."
put offadiar"Don't put off your tasks until the last minute."
break offinterromper"He hung up the phone abruptly."

Phrasal VerbSignificadoExemplo real
